The \"yellow sweet spot Zone\" is just part of the Flow channel.<br />\n<br />\nWhen i was in 9th Standard of school, I was representing my school at the District schools sports meet in 200 metres dash . &nbsp;The standard of athletics in my state of Kerala is the best in the whole of India.<br />\n<br />\nThere were to be 8 heats, and i was 2nd in my own heat. The problem was , that some over aged athletes were participating in my younger Intermediate group, by fudging their age group.. <br />\n<br />\nI had NOT yet started to shave, but most of the guys who were participating along with me had rough stubbles and hairy armpits.<br />\n<br />\nThe guy who beat me in the heats was a ugly stocky tribal type of character, and I sort of looked down on him. But i learnt a valuable lesson , from him which i remember even today , after 41 years.<br />\n<br />\nHe was participating in shot put , as he was a very muscular guy. But he was NOT yet in the top 5 after 2 throws. So i psyched him \" You look, stronger than the others, then why are lagging at 6th position? \"<br />\n<br />\nHe said \" I have my 100 metres finals coming up, now. I will come first in this race, then run over here , and throw for Gold in shot put. I will be in a STATE OF FLOW \".<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-T7YSCebMz1w/TWerGt1eFGI/AAAAAAAADrg/6r54p2Rml9A/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-T7YSCebMz1w/TWerGt1eFGI/AAAAAAAADrg/6r54p2Rml9A/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nI was amazed at his confidence.<br />\n<br />\nSo i watched him win the gold in the 100 metres dash in bare feet , and watched him run up to the shot put pit, and throw the metal ball so far ahead of the competition, that the contest was dead!.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-YfmAe3h-YB4/TWetW9QfYBI/AAAAAAAADrk/RhygWVc-07U/s1600/download.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-YfmAe3h-YB4/TWetW9QfYBI/AAAAAAAADrk/RhygWVc-07U/s1600/download.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nTo cut a long story shot, this boy got the gold in the 200 metres too, and I managed to secure the bronze.<br />\n<br />\nSince then I knew what it means to be IN THE FLOW from a gorilla type, no class, tribal boy.<br />\n<br />\nI am grateful to him. This post is dedicated to him.<br />\n<br />\nIn a state of flow, self consciousness disappears. You are too involved in the activity and your ego takes a backseat. &nbsp;You feel connected to something larger than yourself. You are on the crest of a intuitive high. It is a paradox, that in this state of flow, by letting go, you strengthen your self. You don't lose mental energy in how you appear to others. Time flies and your sense of time gets distorted.<br />\n<br />\nAfter winning the race, the run up to the shot put pit would have been a sort of victory lap for the gorilla. At this time his left brain lobe will be sleeping , while his right lobe would be spiking like hell, in addition to the chemical adrenaline release. When he lifted the metal ball for the throw, his mind would have been blank,as if he did not exist, and he would be in a sort of ecstatic feel mode.<br />\n<br />\nTHE HALLMARK OF FLOW IS THIS FEELING OF SPONTANEOUS JOY- NAY- RAPTURE.<br />\n<br />\nYour attention is undivided and your awareness merges with your action. You are now inside the waterfall of the flow, highly aligned with the task in hand. There is NIL anxiety.<br />\n<br />\nKnowing how to be in the flow, gives athletes the winning edge. Sports psychology is all about knowing how to trigger this state.<br />\n<br />\nYou know what has to be done, and you are doing it. You are engaged by the challenge , but NOT overwhelmed. You find a good match between the demands of the situation and your own innate ability.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">Grace and peace!</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object width=\"320\" height=\"266\" class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://1.gvt0.com/vi/xo8PFx5OeJ0/0.jpg\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/xo8PFx5OeJ0&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/xo8PFx5OeJ0&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-iVZD50P3yTA/TWeqh6iy69I/AAAAAAAADrY/xbgMTRxXhws/s1600/P4270001.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-iVZD50P3yTA/TWeqh6iy69I/AAAAAAAADrY/xbgMTRxXhws/s320/P4270001.JPG\" width=\"296\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nCAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<br />\n..</div>\n", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Give only on RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Insert one 500-mg suppository rectally. The total dose should not exceed 1 g (2 suppositories) in 24 hours.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Store in a refrigerator at 2-8\u00b0C to prevent deterioration. Remove any wrapping before inserting the suppository. Rectal irritation may occur with continued use.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ampicillin capsules, 250 mg<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: For chest infections, urinary and gastrointestinal infections, and infections of the tonsils<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">and throat. <b>Give only on RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE from a physician.</b><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Recommended for susceptible infections. The usual dosage is 1-2 250-mg capsules or tablets four times a day, up to the total dosage of 3.5 g (14\u00d7250-mg capsules) for one course of treatment.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoBodyText2\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;\">The daily dose of ampicillin should be administered simultaneously with 2-4 500-mg tablets of probenecid (see page 326) to prolong the effective blood concentrations of ampicillin.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Ampicillin, chemically quite similar to penicillin, can cause the same types of allergic reaction, such as anaphylactic reaction and skin rash. <b>Persons allergic to penicillin should be assumed to be allergic to ampicillin.</b> Before administering, determine from the patient, if possible, whether he is allergic to either penicillin or ampicillin. Allergic (anaphylactic) reactions can be severe or even fatal. If the patient is allergic to the drug, RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE should be obtained for an alternative anti-infective treatment. If a reaction occurs, discontinue ampicillin, and give emergency treatment (see Allergic reactions, page 167).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ampicillin may produce other side-effects such as nausea, vomiting, or diarrhoea.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Atropine sulfate injection, 0.5 mg/ml<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Injectable atropine sulfate is included for use as an antidote in the treatment of poisoning by insecticides containing organophosphate or carbamate chemicals as part of their formulation. Get RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE in the event of such poisoning.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: If it is determined that one of the above-mentioned poisons is involved, atropine sulfate should be administered at once to prevent coma, cyanosis, or convulsions. In organophosphate or carbamate poisoning, 2-3 mg should be given subcutaneously at once, followed by 1 mg every 15 minutes, until the skin is flushed and dry, or the pulse is mild and rapid. <b>If cyanosis (bluish discoloration of skin) occurs, oxygen should also be administered.<o:p></o:p></b></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: The above doses, which are needed to counteract the poison, result in dry, flushed, or warm skin, dryness of the mouth, rapid pulse, and rapid breathing. These symptoms may lead to restlessness, hallucinations, and disorientation, followed by depression, medullary paralysis, and death. Do not administer this drug before obtaining RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Calamine lotion, plain<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: For relieving itching or irritated skin, heat rash, and hives. Shake the bottle well. Wet a pad of cotton with the lotion and pat it on the affected area.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Do not use on open or \"weeping\" sores,<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Calcium gluconate, effervescent tablets, 1 g<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: This medicament is intended to be used primarily in cases of poisoning by oxalic acid or<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">sodium fluoride. This sort of poisoning may cause a depletion of the calcium content of the blood, resulting in convulsions. Calcium gluconate acts by restoring needed calcium to the blood,<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoBodyText2\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><u><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;\">: Dissolve 5 tablets in 250 ml of water, to be drunk immediately.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">INTERNATIONAL MARITIME ORGANIZATION. Medical first aid guide for use in accidents involving dangerous goods. London, IMO, 1985.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Charcoal, activated, powder<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: In the initial treatment of most poisonings (because of its property to adsorb many poisons).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: 10 g (2 tablespoonfuls). Mix the powder with water prior to administration. Repeat if the patient vomits,<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Note</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Activated charcoal is a general antidote. It should not be used in place of the specific antidote for a poison when that antidote is available (see Chapter 2, page 53). It should not be used on unconscious patients, because of the danger of aspiration of the powder.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: For treating allergic reactions, such as hay fever, urticaria, and anaphylactic shock (in addition to other measures).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: 1 tablet, one to three times daily,<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The patient's ability to work may be impaired. Alcoholic drinks increase the likelihood of side-<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">effects.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Do not give to patients with a history of glaucoma, asthma, or peptic ulcer; consult the doctor<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">before giving it to pregnant women or to children.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Chlorphenamine maleate injection, 10 mg in 1 ml<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: See previous item. May be given subcutaneously or intramuscularly.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: 1 to 2 injections a day.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: (1) For treatment of severe agitation, including acute alcohol withdrawal states and convulsions (epilepsy); (2) may be useful for shivering due to generalized hypothermia, see page 262.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"> Overdosage leads to fatigue, drowsiness, diminished reflexes, dizziness, mental confusion, and coma. It should not be given with sedative preparations or narcotics, as it may intensify sedation. Side-effects with normal dosages may include dryness of the mouth, subnormal body temperature, fever, slurred speech, or visual disturbances in a very few persons. The dosage should be adjusted or the medicament discontinued, if these symptoms occur.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The drug should be given with extreme caution to persons prone to drug abuse.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Warning</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: A controlled substance. Keep an exact record of its use. Store in a locked cabinet,<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Diazepam tablets, 5 mg<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: (1) For treatment of common anxiety and tension, and (2) for the management of agitation during alcohol withdrawal.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Varies from 2 to 10 mg, 2-4 times a day, depending upon the condition being treated.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Overdosage leads to fatigue, drowsiness, light-headedness, diminished reflexes, dizziness, mental confusion, and coma. Patients exhibiting drowsiness should not be allowed to work complicated machinery or stand watch.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoBodyText2\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;\">Other precautions as far diazepam injections, see previous item.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Warning</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: The same as for diazepam injections, see previous Item.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Dimercaprol injections, 50 mg/ml, 2-ml (= 100-mg) ampoules<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: The drug is used as an antidote in poisoning. Indicated in the treatment of arsenic (pesticides), gold, and mercury poisonings; also in acute lead poisoning, in combination with calcium disodium edetate. Always obtain RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE in the event of such poisoning.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Recommended dosage (in adults)</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: If general symptoms of poisoning occur, give dimercaprol,<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">200 mg intramuscularly every 6 hours for the first day, every 8 hours on the second day, and then twice a day for 3 days. Injections should be deep into the muscle; the site of injection should be changed at each administration.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Adverse reactions to this medicament include: headache, nausea, vomiting, abdominal pain; pain and sterile abscesses at injection sites; raised blood pressure and excessively rapid heart action (the blood pressure and pulse rate will return to normal within 2 hours).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ephedrine sulfate capsules, 25 mg<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: (1) To relieve difficult breathing in asthma; (2) to prevent asthmatic attacks in chronic cases (effects appear 30-60 minutes after administration); and (3) to relieve nasal congestion in hay fever and severe head colds. Obtain RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE before using this drug.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: One 25-mg capsule four times a day. If ephedrine is used for several days, phenobarbital may be indicated to overcome its stimulant effects (one 30-mg phenobarbital tablet up to three times a day).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Adverse effects include tremors, heart palpitation, mental anxiety, insomnia, and headache. The drug should not be given to patients with chronic heart disease, high blood pressure, glaucoma, diabetes, or hyperthyroidism. It may cause urinary retention in older men.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Epinephrine hydrochloride injection, 1:1000, 1 ml<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: (1) For acute asthma attacks and for severe allergic reactions to penicillin and other drugs, and to insect bites; (2) for cardiac or circulatory failure.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: By subcutaneous or intramuscular injection, 0.3 ml of 1:1000 solution, every 2<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">hours as necessary. The usual dosage range is 0.1-0.5 ml in asthma, and up to 1 ml in other<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">conditions.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Epinephrine may cause anxiety, heart palpitation, and headache. Excessive doses can cause acute hypertension and irregular heartbeat. Except in life-threatening situations, it should not be administered to patients with hypertension, diabetes, hyperthyroidism, or heart disease.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Erythromycin tablets, 250 mg<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: For a variety of infections of the upper and lower respiratory tract; infections of the mouth, gums, and teeth; infections of the nose, ears and sinuses. Give this antibiotic only when RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE has been received from a physician. It may be useful for patients allergic to penicillin, and for some infections resistant to penicillin.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: One 250-mg tablet, four times a day (for serious infections, dosage may be increased to two 250-mg tablets, four times a day) -to be continued for 48 hours or more after symptoms have subsided.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Occasionally, a skin rash may develop that will require discontinuation of the drug. If the drug is discontinued because of a sensitivity reaction, RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE on alternative therapy should be obtained. Sometimes abdominal discomfort, cramping, or nausea and vomiting may occur; these complaints usually diminish as therapy continues. The drug should not be given to people known to be sensitive to it.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoBodyText3\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Eye anaesthetic drops (0.5% solution of tetracaine hydrochloride)<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: For local anaesthesia of the eye, before removing foreign bodies. Damaged-abraded or ulcerated-corneal tissue absorbs the dye, and the lesion appears greenish or yellowish. Foreign bodies are surrounded by a green ring.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Dosage and administration</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Anaesthetize the eye with one drop of 0.5% tetracaine hydrochloride eye-drops. Remove the fluorescein strip from the sterile wrapper without touching the dyed end. Moisten the dyed end with sterile eye-irrigating solution, Lift the upper eyelid and touch the dyed tip of the strip to the outside corner of the eye; allow the dye to flow across the eye. The patient should close the eyelid tightly after application, to distribute the stain.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Before using the strip, if the eye is dry, instil a drop of sterile eyewash solution.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><h2 style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;\">Furosemide tablets, 40 mg<o:p></o:p></span></h2><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Furosemide is a potent short-acting diuretic, which causes the production of urine by affecting the kidneys. It is indicated in the treatment of excess body fluid (oedema) associated with congestive heart failure, cirrhosis of the liver, or certain kidney diseases.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: The usual oral dosage for adults is 20-80 mg in a single dose in the morning, for 2-4 consecutive days each week, followed by a drug-free period. However, the dosage will vary, depending on the disease and the patient's response.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: This drug should be used only after getting RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE. The doctor will advise on the dosage and on possible side-effects. If excessive doses are administered, there is a rapid loss of sodium, potassium, and calcium electrolytes, in addition to water. The drug is contraindicated in women of child-bearIns age.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Hydrocortisone sodium succinate for injection, 100 mg<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: USE ON MEDICAL ADVICE ONLY: (1) for severe shock-large doses, combined with standard methods of combating shock, help restore blood pressure and circulation; (2) for acute allergic reactions-after epinephrine (or other substances that elevate blood pressure)-to combat severe asthma, drug reactions, and anaphylactic reactions (for example, to penicillin); and (3) for the control of life-threatening inflammation of the lungs after a patient has inhaled vomit (aspiration pneumonitis). Exceptionally, in a case of anaphylactic shock, when there is no time to obtain RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE, 100 mg of this drug may be given intramuscularly.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage and administration</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Dosage depends on the type and severity of the condition. The dose may be as low as 20 mg per day to suppress inflammation, or as high as 2.5 g or more in severe shock. Administer intramuscularly or intravenously, strictly following the doctor's instructions.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Not for patients with ulcerated corneas, acute psychoses, or a history of active or inactive tuberculosis, except in special life-threatening situations. Use with caution in patients with a history of stomach ulcers, in patients suffering from infections, and in the presence of diabetes, hypertension, glaucoma, convulsive disorders, and chronic renal diseases.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Hydrocortisone ointment, 1%<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: For temporary relief of certain skin disorders, common rashes, inflamed skin, and disorders causing itching and discomfort. It may be used for temporary relief of itching, burning, and soreness from haemorrhoids (piles).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Apply a thin film to the affected skin 2-4 times a day, Apply sparingly and with gentle rubbing. Clean the skin before each use.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Warning</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">:<b> Do not apply to the eyes. Do not use for extended periods of time without a physician's order.</b></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"> Discontinue use, if the condition gets worse. This ointment should not be administered to patients with chickenpox, or to people suffering from general infections.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ichthyol and glycerine ointment<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: For treatment of boils, fishermen's hand infections, salt-water boils, etc.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Apply once a day to the affected area.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Morphine sulfate injection, 10 mg/ml, 1 ml<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: For severe pain not relieved by other analgesics. <b>Obtain RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE prior to use.</b> Discontinue as soon as the pain can be relieved by other drugs that can be given orally and are less addictive.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Action of morphine</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">:<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u25a0 relieves pain, calms the mind, reduces restlessness<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u25a0 depresses breathing and coughing<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u25a0 slows the heart rate<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u25a0 slows normal gut movements<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u25a0 may initially cause vomiting.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: For the relief of severe pain following injuries or burns, and severe pain of sudden origin in the abdomen or chest, give 10-15 mg intramuscularly. If the pain is unrelieved, or if it recurs soon after the first dose, a second dose of 10 mg intramuscularly may be given 1 hour or more later. Give further doses, if necessary, at intervals of at least 4 hours-not sooner. If the patient is to be transferred within 4 hours of receiving morphine, note the time and dosage on a tag securely tied to the front part of the patient's clothing.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: An addiction-producing drug.</span></b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"> Do not repeat the injection unless ordered to do so by a physician. Unless the radio medical doctor has instructed you to do so, NEVER GIVE MORPHINE:<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; </span>when the respiratory rate has slowed to less than 12 breaths per minute;<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; tab-stops: 25.0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -24.75pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">(2) <span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>when breathing is difficult (reduced) and the lips and skin are blue, or when the patient has a chest infection or asthma;<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; </span>when mental dullness, unconsciousness, or coma are present, especially after head injury; and<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; tab-stops: 25.0pt; text-align: justify; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Warning</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Morphine sulfate is a controlled substance. Keep an exact record of its use. Keep stock locked away.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Naloxone hydrochloride injection, 0.4 mg/ml, 1 ml<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: For the emergency treatment of respiratory depression resulting from the administration of narcotics, such as morphine. Also indicated for the detection of suspected acute narcotic overdose.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: May be given by subcutaneous, intramuscular, or intravenous injection. The intravenous route of administration is recommended only for emergency situations. The usual dose is 0.4 mg, repeated every 2 or 3 minutes until a favourable response is achieved. If no improvement is noted after 2 or 3 doses, another cause of the depression should be suspected.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Obtain RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE on whether the use of naloxone is indicated.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: The use of naloxone does not preclude that of other resuscitative measures when indicated, such as the maintenance of an adequate airway, artificial respiration, and heart compression. Naloxone is not effective in the treatment of respiratory depression caused by non-narcotic drugs, such as alcoholic beverages, and hypnotics such as phenobarbital.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoBodyText3\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Neomycin + bacitracin ointment (5 mg neomycin + 500 international units bacitracin zinc per gram)<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: In treatment and prevention of infection, in second- and third-degree burns.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: The cream or ointment should be applied to cleansed burnt areas once or twice daily to a thickness of 1-2 mm. Continue as long as there is a possibility of infection, unless a significant adverse reaction occurs.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Local adverse reactions may occur, such as pain, burning, or itching. RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE should be sought to determine whether the drug should be discontinued.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoBodyText3\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Oral rehydration salts, in aluminium bag, sealed (contents of each bag to be dissolved in 1 litre of boiled cooled water)<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: For the treatment of diarrhoea and other diseases causing dehydration.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Give the solution to the patient to drink rapidly, for instance, 1 glass every 5-10 minutes, until the signs of dehydration disappear (see Diarrhoea page 188, and Cholera, page 128). Then give 1 glass after each bowel movement, to replace the continuing loss of water and salts.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Oxygen<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Oxygen is a gas that constitutes about 20% of ordinary air; it is necessary for the maintenance of life.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: To make up for lack of oxygen in blood and tissues, the signs and symptoms or which are cyanosis (bluish colour to skin and nail-beds), dyspnoea (rapid, shallow breathing), rapid,<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">thready pulse, and restlessness. Oxygen may be indicated for respiratory diseases, cardiac diseases, poisoning from gases, massive haemorrhage, and shock.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: The usual adult dose is 6-8 litres per minute by mask; or 5-6 litres per minute by nasal catheter,<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Only trained personnel should administer oxygen. <b>The use of oxygen presents an explosion hazard.</b> In the immediate area, do not allow any smoking, open flames, electrical devices, flammable liquids (such as alcohol and ether), or any device that may cause a spark or is combustible. Compressed oxygen is marketed in metal cylinders; these must be handled carefully to prevent their falling or bumping into each other.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoBodyText3\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Petrolatum (white petroleum jelly)<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: As a bland and neutral protective dressing. Apply to minor burns, abrasions, or dry skin.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Potassium permanganate (crystals), 100 g<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Diluted in water (1 g of crystals to 0.5-1 litre of water). This substance is used for the disinfection of the skin and mucous membranes and for the treatment of some skin diseases.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: The substance (or any highly concentrated dilution of it) is very toxic if ingested.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Salbutamol, aerosol<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: In bronchial asthma, as inhaled spray. The medicament dilates the bronchi and brings quick relief (within several minutes) in an asthmatic attack.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Usually 0.1-0.5 ml (2 puffs) of solution of salbutamol, given as a spray. Closely follow manufacturer's instructions on how to use the spray.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Sodium chloride injection, 0.9%, 500 ml<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Intravenously (1) to replace water chloride, and sodium lost in extensive vomiting or diarrhoea, (2) in dehydration due to excessive sweating, and (3) in mild haemorrhage. <b>Obtain RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE before administering </b>(see page 117).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adult dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Depends on patient's condition, Generally, 1500-3000 ml may be given over 24 hours. Do not give intravenous solutions at a faster rate than 500 ml per hour, except on RADIO MEDICAL ADVICE.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Caution</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: As with any injection, sterile procedures should be observed. Do not administer any intravenous solution unless it is clear and free of particles. Watch the solution carefully while it is being administered. In order to keep air from entering the patient's vein, do not allow the bottle to drain completely of fluid.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoBodyText3\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Zinc oxide paste (Lassar's plain zinc paste)<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: A nontoxic, protective, water-insoluble, mildly astringent, and antiseptic paste employed<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">in a large variety of diseases and irritations of the skin. Zinc oxide paste differs from zinc oxide ointment in that it is somewhat more protective.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Dosage</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">: Apply as needed in a thin layer to skin areas to be treated or protected from sunlight or weather.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoBodyTextIndent\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -55.95pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;
