mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Threshold Limit Value \u2013 Time Weighted Average</span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"> -The Threshold Limit Value Time Weighted average (TLV-TWA) is usually expressed in units of parts per million (ppm) - The TLV is defined as the concentration of the substance in air that can be breathed for five consecutive eight-hour workdays (40-hour work week) by most people without adverse effect . As some people become ill after exposure to concentrations lower than the TLV, this value cannot be used to define exactly what is a \"safe\" or \"dangerous\" concentration.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">No entry appears when the chemical is a mixture; it is possible to calculate the TLV for a mixture only when the TLV for each component of the mixture is known and the composition of the mixture by weight is also known.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Threshold Limit Value - Short-Term Exposure Limits</span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"> - The parts of vapor (gas per million parts of contaminated air by volume at 25<sup>o</sup>C (77<sup>o</sup>F) and one atmosphere pressure is given. The limits are given in milligrams per cubic meter for chemicals that can form a fine mist or dust. The values given are the maximum permissible average exposures for the time periods specified. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Threshold Limit Value \u2013 Ceiling Value</span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"> \u2013 The parts of vapor (gas per million parts of contaminated air by volume at 25<sup>o</sup>C (77<sup>o</sup>F) and one atmosphere pressure is given. The limits are given in milligrams per cubic meter for chemicals that can form a fine mist or dust. The values given are for a concentration that is not to be exceeded at any time.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">OSHA puts TLV of Benzene at 1 ppm<span style=\"color: black;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Toxicity by Ingestion</span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"> - The Grade and corresponding LD<sub>50</sub> value are those defined by the National Academy of Sciences, Committee on Hazardous Materials, \"Evaluation of the Hazard of Bulk Water Transportation of Industrial Chemicals, A Tentative Guide,\" Washington, D.C., 1972. Data were also collected from other sources and converted to the appropriate Grade before entry in this manual. The term LD<sub>50</sub> signifies that about 50% of the animals given the specified dose by mouth will die. Thus, for a Grade 4 chemical (below 50 mg/kg) the toxic dose for 50% of animals weighing 70 kg (150 lb) is 70 X 50 = 3500 mg = 3.5 g, or less than 1 teaspoonful; it might be as little as a few drops. For a Grade 1 chemical (5 to 15g/k g), the LD<sub>50</sub> would be between a pint and a quart for a 150-lb man. All LD<sub>50</sub> values have been obtained using small laboratory animals such as rodents, cats, and dogs. The substantial risks taken in using these values for estimating human toxicity are the same as those taken when new drugs are administered to humans for the first time.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Toxicity by Inhalation</span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"> \u2013 Similar to the Toxicity by Ingestion entry, except that the route of exposure is inhalation instead of ingestion. Units and definition of units are the same.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Chronic Toxicity</span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"> - Where there is evidence that the chemical can cause cancer, mutagenic effects, teratogenic effects, or a delayed injury to vital organs such as the liver or kidney, a qualitative description of the effect is given.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Odor Threshold</span></b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"> - This is the lowest concentration in air that most humans can detect by smell. The value cannot be relied on to prevent over-exposure, because human sensitivity to odors varies over wide limits, some chemicals cannot be smelled at toxic concentrations, odors can be masked by other odors, and some compounds rapidly deaden the sense of smell<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">IDLH Value</span></b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"> - The Immediately Dangerous to Life and Health Value - This concentration represents a maximum level from which one could escape within 30 minutes without any escape-impairing symptoms or any irreversible health effects. The concentrations are reported in either parts per million (ppm) or milligrams per cubic meter (mg/m<sup>3</sup>).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "3", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/715192582118073177/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "8342926757527217055", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2011-02-25T14:52:00+05:30", "updated": "2018-07-30T20:46:01+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxNTMyOTYzNzYxMjg2Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/02/speed-reading-capt-ajit-vadakayil.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/8342926757527217055", "title": "SPEED READING -- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-wHI0NpWYCWU/TWd0B2CEI1I/AAAAAAAADq8/chZfJ25CTHY/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-wHI0NpWYCWU/TWd0B2CEI1I/AAAAAAAADq8/chZfJ25CTHY/s1600/images.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nCouple of years ago, my stainless steel tanker was chartered by the world's No 1 oil major ( no names ). <br />\n<br />\nThe ship used to discharge Gasoline , Jet fuel and Diesel at several ports of an Island country.<br />\n<br />\nI was due to hand over command, and I felt that 2 of the minor ports ( where I had discharged twice ) were unsafe for my ship -- so i made a iron clad risk assessment using my own format and declared the ports as unsafe , as the ship was too large --an absolute NO GO--NYET !!<br />\n<br />\nAs soon as I sent this, &nbsp;the charterers were forced to act, &nbsp;and one of these ports was skipped.<br />\n<br />\nThere was immediate hue and cry as the whole area was starved of fuel. &nbsp;There were huge write ups in the local newspapers, and I was the bad guy.<br />\n<br />\nAt the next port, I was told to go ashore and meet the owner of the Charterer's agency--an European. As I stepped into his office , I could see from his body language that he was pretending to read something. I sat on a chair and patiently waited , sensing the hostility.<br />\n<br />\nPretty soon, he asked me to take a chair at his desk, no shake hands, no usual protocol courtesies.<br />\n<br />\nHe gave me a newspaper and told that my ship and I , occupied the front page, with almost all the big shots and ministers commenting on the crisis, caused by the Captain of the ship, not playing ball--and how the unsafe port was indeed very safe etc.<br />\n<br />\nI read the article and gave it back to him.<br />\n<br />\nHe said \" WHAAA-- captain, you have not even read what i told you to !. Reading this entire thing will take at least 10 times more time than you took. &nbsp;Probably they are right in saying, that you have an attitude problem? \"<br />\n<br />\nI said \" Well, I have read it, and if you feel I have not read it , you can ask me questions based on the article!\"<br />\n<br />\nHe immediately ask me a few questions. <br />\n<br />\nAnd he was amazed that I could answer all of it. After he had finished I said \" Now you can ask me about the other headlines on the same page-- choose your pick!\"<br />\n<br />\nThis man suddenly turned from foe to friend. He jumped up and wanted to shake my hand and hug me .<br />\n<br />\nHe said that he has never seen anything like this before--and then he insisted that he wants to have a drink with me and dinner too.<br />\n<br />\nWe became good friends over dinner, and he had several intelligent questions to ask me about speed reading , as well as some advise on some personal matters.<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">Now I have to digress.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">Once i told my second engineer , (who wanted to know how my memory is so sharp ), that I see words as pictures.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">He immediately cried \" I have named my new born son, Tamil Selvan. What picture do you see?\".</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">I said \" Imagine a deer is taking a crap-- when the last ounce of s#it is poppin' out of its a$$hole-- imagine you smear this gooey mass with your thumb, all over the orifice. Well that is word Tamil Selvan in my minds eye !\"</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">Needless to say, though I told him the truth, I lost one of my ardent fans, on the spot.</span><br />\n<br />\n<i>Once at a Chemical course, the lecturer made the students read the IBC code paras , one by one. And then the stupid man would ask \" Understood?\"</i><br />\n<i><br />\n</i><br />\n<i>I jumped up and said \" Well all have understood except the reader, for he was more concerned about his verbal pronunciation. &nbsp;If you don't believe me ask any reader , about what he read!\"</i><br />\n<i><br />\n</i><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-5wuVQvziH6Q/TWd0NYWKBBI/AAAAAAAADrA/Q4ZpypBdyCk/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-5wuVQvziH6Q/TWd0NYWKBBI/AAAAAAAADrA/Q4ZpypBdyCk/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nWell back to business--<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">SPEED READERS DRINK INFORMATION THROUGH THE EYES</span>--PERIOD!<br />\n<br />\nIt is a mysterious right brain lobe ( for right handers ) powered , eye and mind method.--where the eye is the gate to the mind.<br />\n<br />\nMouth and ears are out castes.<br />\n<br />\nIt is important to be comfortable with the font . The letter size should NOT be in capitals ( upper case ).<br />\n<br />\nYou yourself can try to read a page on small case, and then convert it to large size upper case, and see how your brain rejects the information.<br />\n<br />\nIn speed reading the eyes directed by the mind, does not give importance to 60% of the words. The mind directs the eyes to the key words and then later the mind fills up the blanks itself.<br />\n<br />\nA little bit of peripheral vision is also involved. Like when you drive a car in a busy street , the subconscious mind registers what the eye does not-- and you are safe. You don't knock down the motorcycles in total chaos around you.<br />\n<br />\nWhile speed reading, your eyes move steadily, like a train on a track, never going in reverse.<br />\n<br />\nThe mind does not care for the words. It gulps in passages. The mind set is such, that you are NOT afraid of missing out anything.<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">There is a holographic Gamma wave synthesis inside the brain. You are in a new dimension of consciousness--where you mind is totally in the present. EEG will register &gt;40 Hertz.</span><br />\n<br />\nIn this quantum act, there is hardly any trade off between speed and comprehension like the classical quality / quantity lever on a fulcrum.<br />\n<br />\nThe mind sees the multitude of words as ore, it just sucks in the gold.<br />\n<br />\nTry it!<br />\n<br />\nSurprised?<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-_cluamJwFpM/TWd0kDSlp4I/AAAAAAAADrE/6UUXjp0p5IY/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-_cluamJwFpM/TWd0kDSlp4I/AAAAAAAADrE/6UUXjp0p5IY/s400/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" width=\"284\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; float: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n<img src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-0Gvy5mBcipE/WlAJZNfU3zI/AAAAAAABXsU/wZaBJr4cOoclmnshY0dz6Y3NbokDpLaaACK4BGAYYCw/s35/*\" style=\"background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1) 1px 1px 5px; max-width: 36px; padding: 5px;\" /></div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c1656624571752202381\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 17.6px; margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_153M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"font-size: 16px; margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user blog-author\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">Capt. style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Path: \\MASTER\\SentBox<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Sub : Re: TECH -- ME Safety filter<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">SOME THEORY FOR ENGINEERS WHO WRONGLY BELIEVE THAT RIGOROUS AND&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">CONTINIOUS PURIFICATION CAN REMOVE POLYMER STRANDS,</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">ROGUE POLYMER STRAND : a polymer strand of smallest size 35 microns which escapes centrifuging because its density is only around 650 kg/ m3 while the 380 cst HO is 990 kg/ m3-- asphaltenes and the polymers agglomerates into a sticky gooey ,due to static charges inherited while centrifuging --<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Centrifugal force is directly proportional to the radius and to the mass, but it is also proportional to the square of the angular velocity. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">For example, doubling the mass of the rotating object will increase the centrifugal force by a factor of 2, but doubling the number of revolutions per minute (rpm) will increase the centrifugal force by a factor of 4 (equals 2 times 2); similarly, increasing the speed by a factor of 10 will increase the force by a factor of 100 (equals 10 times 10)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">centrifugal force is expressed by the basic relation F = m\u00ed2 / R = 4\u00f02mn2R; F is the centrifugal force, m the mass, R the radius, v the speed, and n the number of revolutions per second.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">suspended particles denser than the suspending liquid tend to migrate toward the periphery, while those LESS DENSE LIKE OUR NOT SO FRIENDLY POLYMER FINE STRANDS MOVE TOWARDS THE CENTRE ALONG WITH THE PURIFIED&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">FUEL.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The rapidity with which the migration proceeds is dependent on the intensity of the centrifugal field, the difference between the density of the particle and that of the suspending liquid, the viscosity of the liquid, the size and shape of the particle, and to some extent the concentration of the particles and the degree to which they are electrically charged.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The net motivating force exerted on the particle is the difference between the centrifugal field acting on it and the opposing buoyancy of the liquid. All other things being equal for two particles, one with a diameter 10 times that of the other will require only 1/100 as much average centrifugal field to move a given distance in a given time as the smaller.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">an experiment for the advocaters of rigorous and continious purification: a partial separation of two groups of suspended particles of different size can be effected by allowing centrifugation to continue--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">ONLY LONG ENOUGH for all of the larger particles to be completely packed into the sediment, since then many of the small particles will still be suspended in the fluid. If separation of the smaller particles is desired, the surface fluid can be drawn off and the sediment resuspended in some suitable liquid and subsequently centrifuged again to effect further separation-or you must go for vacuum type tubular centrifuges NOT available on board ships. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">vacuum type : the density-gradient vacuum centrifuge consists in setting up a radial density variation or gradient in the tubular centrifuge with slowly sedimenting nonreactive smaller molecules&nbsp; If, then, the density of the substance to be purified falls within the range of the artificial density gradient, it will collect in a thin cylindrical surface at a definite radius. If more than one substance is in the solution, each of the substances will collect at a radius determined by its particle density.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">and pray--why go fo all this? It was compulsory to experiment on real human cadavers. He allowed lower caste Hindus into his school ( unlike Charaka )-- so that the higher castes who were squeamish to handle dead bodies could be exempted. Suturing would be done with compatible animal organic threads, which did NOT require removal. .<br />\n<br />\nEven today , 6000 years later , the Ayurveda stalwarts in Kerala Dhanwantari colleges are NOT from Brahmins or higher castes.&nbsp; Sushruta used alcohol and opium for anesthesia.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-r1bsTRr7V_g/TWaH06VAk7I/AAAAAAAADqU/wo8b9nhUZXw/s1600/download+%25284%2529.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-r1bsTRr7V_g/TWaH06VAk7I/AAAAAAAADqU/wo8b9nhUZXw/s320/download+%25284%2529.JPG\" width=\"246\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Sustruta's surgery\ntexts and leech therapy were known to the Arabs, who traded with Kerala . Arabs\ndid not steal the work. It was given to them free. The Europeans ( Greeks and\nItalians )stole the knowledge from the Arabs,and patented it for themselves in\nLatin. Knowledge thief and Free Mason&nbsp;\nEdward Jenner stole the vedic vaccination idea and patented it in his\nname.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; Adding certain microbes to our internal ecosystem can help in the treatment of these problems as well as in treating some forms of autism.<br />\n<br />\nProbiotics don\u2019t always colonize the gut and could even slow down recovery of the gut microbiome after antibiotics<br />\n<br />\nhttp://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2013/08/probiotics-prebiotics-friendly-gut.html<br />\n<br />\nAn altered gut microbiome is associated with a number of different chronic diseases, including , diabetes, metabolic syndrome, inflammatory bowel disease (IBD), irritable bowel syndrome (IBS), skin conditions, anxiety, depression, and multiple sclerosis, to name a few.<br />\n<br />\n70% of physicians regularly prescribe probiotics to their patients.. Probiotics are widely used and prescribed during or after antibiotics, with the idea that flooding the system with good bacteria can help prevent the adverse effects of antibiotic-induced gut dysbiosis<br />\n<br />\nThe gut can be divided into the upper GI tract (small intestine) and the lower GI tract (large intestine, or colon). It can also be divided cross-sectionally into the gut lumen and the gut mucosa. If you think of the gut as a hollow tube, the lumen is the innermost (center) part of the tube, while the mucosa is like a sticky gel-like substance coating the wall of the tube.<br />\n<br />\nSo we can think of the G.I. tract as a hollow tube, and all the inside walls of that tube are coated with this thick, protective gel. And so in this analogy, the gel represents the gut mucus layer, and the very inner center of that tube represents the gut lumen. And each of these regions has a distinct community of microbes, but these are rarely studied because these regions are rather inaccessible unless you undergo invasive endoscopy.<br />\n<br />\nThe human microbiome can take many months to recover from a single course of broad-spectrum antibiotics, and even then, recovery may be incomplete. Antibiotic exposure, especially during the early years of life, is associated with an increased risk of developing allergies, asthma, autoimmunity, obesity, IBD, and skin conditions. A mass extinction, is caused by broad-spectrum antibiotics, which significantly alter community dynamics<br />\n<br />\nIn reality treating the gut with probiotics actually delayed the normal recovery process of the gut microbiome. Most probiotic products today are developed with Bifidobacteria, Lactobacilli, and other lactic acid bacteria, such as Lactococci and Streptococci who prevent microbiota recovery..<br />\n<br />\nAncient Ayurveda used nano silver and nano gold to selectively and intelligently target harmful bacteria and viruses \u2013based on electric charge ..<br />\n<br />\nPeople who take high doses of antibiotics tend to lose many of their normal gut bacteria, allowing a naturally antibiotic-resistant species called Clostridium difficile to overgrow and cause severe gastric problems, especially chronic diarrhea.<br />\n<br />\nCONTINUED TO 2--</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-replies\" style=\"margin-left: 36px; margin-top: 1em;\">\n<div class=\"comment-thread inline-thread\" id=\"c4736503402384504379-rt\" style=\"background-color: #eeeeee; margin: 8px 0px; padding: 0.5em 1em;\">\n<ol class=\"thread-chrome thread-expanded\" id=\"c4736503402384504379-ra\" style=\"list-style-type: none; padding: 0px;\">\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"c4346019654972987138\" style=\"border-bottom: 0px; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 16px 0px 0px;\"><div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"float: left; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">Capt. margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">\u201cThis life of yours which you are living is not merely a piece of this entire existence,</span></i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;<i>but in a certain sense the whole; only this whole is not so constituted that it can be&nbsp;surveyed in one single glance. This, as we know, is what the Brahmins express in that&nbsp;sacred, mystic formula which is yet really so simple and so clear; <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: large;\"><b>tat tvam asi</b></span>,</span>&nbsp;this is&nbsp;you. , serif;\">\u092c\u094d\u0930\u0939\u094d\u092e\u0948\u0935\u0947\u0926\u092e\u092e\u0943\u0924\u0902</span></i><i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></i><i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;mangal&quot; , serif;\">\u092a\u094d\u0930\u0938\u0943\u0924\u0902</span></i><i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></i><i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;mangal&quot; , serif;\">\u092c\u094d\u0930\u0939\u094d\u092e\u0948\u0935\u0947\u0926\u0902</span></i><i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></i><i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;mangal&quot; , serif;\">\u0935\u093f\u0936\u094d\u0935\u092e\u093f\u0926\u0902</span></i><i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></i><i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;mangal&quot; , serif;\">\u0965</span></i><i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;2.2.11&nbsp;</span></i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-79WqQJZTrkM/TWZLwndkFRI/AAAAAAAADoQ/L5eBEVf_Vb0/s1600/images+%252819%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Schrodinger&nbsp;&nbsp;speaking of a universe based on super-imposed inseparable waves of probability amplitudes&nbsp;-- \u201cThe unity and continuity of Vedanta are reflected in the unity and continuity of&nbsp;wave</span></i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;<i>mechanics. &nbsp;This is entirely consistent with the Vedanta concept of All in One.\u201d</i><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Schrodinger's biographer Moore, &nbsp;wrote -- \u201cHis system \u2013 or that of the Upanishads \u2013 is</span></i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;<i>delightful and consistent: the self and the world are one and they are all. He rejected&nbsp;traditional western religious beliefs (Jewish, Christian, and Islamic) not on the basis of&nbsp;any reasoned argument, nor even with an expression of emotional antipathy, for he&nbsp;loved to use religious expressions and metaphors, but simply by saying that they are&nbsp;na\u00efve--and will NOT understand Quantum theory and consciousness.</i><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In a famous essay on determinism and free will,&nbsp;he expressed very clearly the sense</span></i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;<i>that consciousness is a unity, arguing that this &nbsp; \u201cinsight is not new\u2026From the early&nbsp;great Upanishads the recognition Atman = Brahman (the personal self equals the&nbsp;omnipresent, all-comprehending eternal self) was in Indian thought considered, far&nbsp;from being blasphemous, to represent, the quintessence of deepest insight into the&nbsp;happenings of the world. The striving of all the scholars of Vedanta was, after havinglearnt to pronounce with their lips, really to assimilate in their minds this grandest of&nbsp;all thoughts.\u201d</i><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Schrodinger wrote:</span></i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;<i>\u201cVedanta teaches that consciousness is singular, all happenings are played out in&nbsp;one universal consciousness and&nbsp;<b>there is no multiplicity of selves</b>.\u201d\u201cthe stages of human development are to strive for Possession (Artha), Knowledge&nbsp;(Dharma), Ability (Kama), Being (Moksha)\u201d&nbsp;\u201cNirvana is a state of pure blissful knowledge..&nbsp;It has nothing to do with individual.&nbsp;The ego or its separation is an illusion.&nbsp;The goal of man is to preserve his Karma and&nbsp;to develop it further \u2013 when man dies his karma lives and creates for itself another&nbsp;carrier.\u201d</i><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">\u201cIn all world,\u201d writes Schroedinger in his book My View of the World (chapter iv),&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">\u201cthere is no kind of framework within which we can find consciousness in the plural;&nbsp;this is simply something we construct because of the temporal plurality of&nbsp;individuals, but it is a false construction\u2026.The only solution to this conflict in so far as&nbsp; any is available to us at all lies in the ancient wisdom of the Upanishad.\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">(source: My View of the World \u2013 By Erwin Schroedinger chapter iv).<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Schroedinger explicitly affirmed his conviction that&nbsp;Vedantic jnana represented the&nbsp; only true view of reality- a view for which he was prepared even to offer Empirical&nbsp;proof. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">(source: A Short Introduction to Hinduism \u2013 By Klaus K. Klostermaier p. 168).<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Regarding mystical insights, Schrodinger tells us: \u201cThe multiplicity is only apparent.&nbsp;This is the doctrine of the Upanishads. And not of the Upanishads only. The mystical&nbsp;experience of the union with God regularly leads to this view, unless strong&nbsp;prejudices stand in the West.\u201d&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">(source: The Eye of Shiva: Eastern Mysticism and Science \u2013 By Amaury de Riencourt &nbsp;p.78).<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In autumn of 1925 Schrodinger wrote an interestingly personal account of his&nbsp;philosophy of life (Mein Welten sicht \u2013 My World View).&nbsp;</span></i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">He completed this only in&nbsp;1960 and in chapter 5 of this book he gives the basic view of Vedanta. He writes-\u201cVedanta teaches that consciousness is singular, all happenings are played out in one&nbsp;</span></i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">universal consciousness and there is no multiplicity of selves.&nbsp;</span></i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-eH9s2HpnMzk/TWZPYgCSY1I/AAAAAAAADpo/BEBQZkCzACQ/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-eH9s2HpnMzk/TWZPYgCSY1I/AAAAAAAADpo/BEBQZkCzACQ/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Maya is the material cause of this world. In all the apparently individual form of existence the individual Brahman is present. Schrodinger did not believe that it will be possible to demonstrate the unity of consciousness by logical arguments. One must make imaginative leap guided by communion with nature and the persuasion of&nbsp; analogies.&nbsp;</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">While&nbsp;scientists like Schrodinger did not possess a direct knowledge of Sanskrit to discern&nbsp;first hand both the letter and spirit of Upanishads, there are persons like Robert&nbsp;Oppenheimer who were not lacking in such an advantage. The fact is that&nbsp;irrespective of east or west, the great minds everywhere have perceived that the&nbsp;ultimate reality remains timeless and changeless.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Nobel Prize Laureates Nils Bohr and Erwin Schroedinger, the founders of quantum physics, were both convinced that quantum processes are the interface between consciousness and matter.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 11.25pt;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The Upanishads were collectively considered amongst the&nbsp;100 most influential books ever written by eminent people like Thoreau, Kant, Schopenhauer, Schrodinger, Werner Heisenberg , Tesla, Einstein etc.<o:p></o:p></span></i><br />\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; You have known neither paradise nor hell. Here there is no happiness, no punishment, no family, no enemies. Rise in tranquility. Here words end, like thought. Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2017/12/comments-overflow-for-inoperative-load_30.html?showComment=1514595161341#c2849351715198825203\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888;\">December 30, 2017 at 6:22 AM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_7MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nCONTINUED FROM 2-<br />\n<br />\nEntanglement involves putting objects in the peculiar limbo of quantum superposition, in which an object's quantum properties occupy multiple states at once<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/02/schrodinger-father-of-quantum-physics.html</span><br />\n<br />\nPhysicists have entangled particles such as electrons and photons, as well as larger objects such as superconducting electric circuits.<br />\n<br />\nTheoretically, even if entangled objects are separated, their precarious quantum states should remain linked until one of them is measured or disturbed. That measurement instantly determines the state of the other object, no matter how far away. The idea is so counterintuitive that IDIOT Albert Einstein mocked it as \"spooky action at a distance.\"<br />\n<br />\nIn 2015, the most sophisticated of these tests, which involved measuring entangled electrons 1.3 kilometers apart, showed once again that spooky action is real.<br />\n<br />\nBeyond the fundamental result, such experiments also point to the possibility of hack-proof communications.<br />\n<br />\nLong strings of entangled photons, shared between distant locations, can be \"quantum keys\" that secure communications. Anyone trying to eavesdrop on a quantum-encrypted message would disrupt the shared key, alerting everyone to a compromised channel.<br />\n<br />\nPSSSSTTT-- BEFORE CHINA INVENTS THE QUANTUM SATELLITE--WE MUST BREAK THE NATION INTO 4 PARTS AND HAVE TIBET AS A NEIGHBOUR<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nEntangled photons degrade rapidly as they pass through the air or optical fibers. So far, the farthest anyone has sent a quantum key is a few hundred kilometers.<br />\n<br />\nOnce you have satellites distributing your quantum signals throughout the globe, you've done it,--You've leapfrogged all the problems you have with losses in fibers.<br />\n<br />\nJian-Wei Pan, a physicist at the University of Science and Technology of China in Shanghai, got the chance to test the idea when the Micius satellite, was launched in August 2016. The satellite is the foundation of the $100 million Quantum Experiments at Space Scale program<br />\n<br />\nBell's theorem is a \"no-go theorem\" that draws an important distinction between quantum mechanics (QM) and the world as described by classical mechanics<br />\n<br />\nIn its simplest form, Bell's theorem states: No physical theory of local hidden variables can ever reproduce all of the predictions of quantum mechanics.<br />\n<br />\nBell's theorem is the most profound discovery of science.and it is lifted straight out of the Vedas<br />\n<br />\nThere is no need for a faster-than-light signal to tell particle A what measurement has been carried out on particle B, because the universe, including particle A, already 'knows' what that measurement, and its outcome, will be.<br />\n<br />\nLOT OF MY DETRACTORS WERE GUFFAWING LIKE DONKEY WHO HAVE SEEN FRESH SHIT WHEN THEY HEARD THAT MY WIFE MATCHED MORE THAN 500 HOROSCOPES FOR MY ELDER SONs BRIDE<br />\n<br />\nBell\u2019s theorem and subsequent experiments proved the so called entanglements to be right. In such cases, two or more atoms, electrons or photons demonstrate correlated properties even at distances where no communication is possible between them during the given time.<br />\n<br />\nThese developments are the most important developments in the history of physics and the whole of science. They agree with Vedanta. They give rise to the idea of the interconnected wholeness of the world and non-local interactions in contrast to the separate identities with local interactions.<br />\n<br />\nIn their first experiment, the Chinese team sent a laser beam into a light-altering crystal on the satellite. The crystal emitted pairs of photons entangled so that their polarization states would be opposite when one was measured.<br />\n<br />\nThe pairs were split, with photons sent to separate receiving stations in Delingha and Lijiang, 1200 kilometers apart. Both stations are in the mountains of Tibet, reducing the amount of air the fragile photons had to traverse., the team reports simultaneously measuring more than 1000 photon pairs.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nCONTINUED TO 4--</div>\n<span class=\"comment-actions secondary-text\" id=\"bc_0_7MN\" kind=\"m\"><span class=\"item-control blog-admin pid-1783552029\" style=\"display: inline;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-replies\" id=\"bc_0_7BR\" style=\"margin-left: 36px; margin-top: 1em;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-replybox-single\" id=\"bc_0_7B_box\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; margin-top: 5px;\">\n</div>\n</li>\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"bc_0_8B\" kind=\"b\" style=\"border-bottom: 0px; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0.25em 0px 0px;\"><div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"float: left; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c5265314992318285551\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_8M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user blog-author\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888;\">Capt. When a property of one of a pair of entangled particles is measured, the other \"immediately\" settles down into a state compatible with that measurement.<br />\n<br />\nSo how fast is \"immediately\"?<br />\n<br />\nAccording to research by Prof. Juan Yin and colleagues at the University of Science and Technology of China in Shanghai, the lower limit to the speed associated with entanglement dynamics \u2013 or \"spooky action at a distance\" \u2013 is at least 10,000 times faster than light.<br />\n<br />\nVedas says INSTANTANEOUSLY<br />\n<br />\nNiels Bohr, one of the prime developers of quantum theory, once said that those who are not shocked when they first encounter quantum theory cannot possibly have understood it.
